General Overview
TINJAUAN MAKROEKONOMI GLOBAL
Tahun 2024 merupakan periode penuh tantangan bagi 
perekonomian global, dipengaruhi oleh meningkatnya 
ketegangan geopolitik, kebijakan moneter ketat di 
negara-negara 
maju, 
serta 
ketidakstabilan 
harga 
komoditas utama yang berdampak pada rantai pasok 
global. Ketidakpastian yang terus membayangi dunia, 
baik dari aspek geopolitik maupun kebijakan ekonomi, 
memberikan tekanan terhadap dinamika pertumbuhan di 
berbagai kawasan.
Laporan World Economic Outlook yang dirilis oleh 
Dana Moneter Internasional (IMF) memperkirakan 
pertumbuhan ekonomi dunia pada tahun 2024 sebesar 
3,3%, lebih rendah dibandingkan rata-rata historis pada 
periode 2000-2019 yang mencapai 3,7%. Di antara 
negara-negara utama, Amerika Serikat menunjukkan 
ketahanan yang lebih kuat dibandingkan kawasan lain, 
sementara Eropa menghadapi ketidakpastian yang 
signifikan, dan perlambatan ekonomi Tiongkok turut 
memberikan tekanan terhadap stabilitas ekonomi global.
Ketatnya kebijakan moneter di negara-negara maju, 
terutama di Amerika Serikat dan Eropa, turut menambah 
tekanan terhadap pasar keuangan global. Suku bunga 
yang tetap tinggi di banyak negara untuk menekan 
inflasi menyebabkan aliran modal keluar dari negara 
berkembang serta meningkatkan volatilitas nilai tukar 
mata uang di berbagai kawasan. Selain itu, harga 
komoditas yang fluktuatif, termasuk minyak dan gas, 
turut memperberat beban ekonomi negara-negara 
pengimpor energi.
Sektor perdagangan internasional juga mengalami 
tekanan akibat ketegangan geopolitik yang meningkat, 
terutama konflik di beberapa kawasan strategis yang 
berdampak pada gangguan rantai pasok global. Hal 
ini menyebabkan lonjakan harga bahan baku dan 
meningkatkan biaya produksi di berbagai industri, 
memperlambat pemulihan ekonomi di banyak negara. 
Dengan situasi yang penuh ketidakpastian ini, kebijakan 
ekonomi global pada tahun 2024 cenderung berfokus 
pada mitigasi risiko dan peningkatan ketahanan ekonomi 
dalam menghadapi guncangan eksternal.
GLOBAL MACROECONOMIC REVIEW
2024 has been a challenging period for the global 
economy, influenced by rising geopolitical tensions, tight 
monetary policies in developed countries, and instability 
in the prices of key commodities, affecting global supply 
chains. Ongoing uncertainty, in terms of geopolitical 
factors and economic policies, has put pressure on 
growth dynamics in various regions.
The World Economic Outlook report released by the 
International Monetary Fund (IMF) forecasts global 
economic growth of 3.3% in 2024, lower than the 
historical average of 3.7% from 2000 to 2019. Among 
major countries, the United States is showing stronger 
resilience compared to other regions, Europe faces 
significant uncertainty, and the economic slowdown 
in China is also putting pressure on global economic 
stability.
Tight 
monetary 
policies 
in 
developed 
countries, 
particularly in the United States and Europe, have added 
pressure to global financial markets. High interest rates 
in many countries, aimed at controlling inflation, have led 
to capital outflows from emerging markets and increased 
currency exchange rate volatility in various regions. 
Additionally, fluctuating commodity prices, including 
oil and gas, have further burdened the economies of 
energy-importing countries.
The international trade sector has also faced pressure 
due to rising geopolitical tensions, particularly conflicts 
in strategic regions that have disrupted global supply 
chains. This has led to a spike in raw material prices and 
increased production costs across various industries, 
slowing economic recovery in many countries. Given this 
uncertain situation, global economic policies in 2024 are 
likely to focus on risk mitigation and enhancing economic 
resilience against external shocks.

TINJAUAN MAKROEKONOMI NASIONAL
Di 
tengah 
kondisi 
global 
yang 
tidak 
menentu, 
perekonomian Indonesia tetap menunjukkan ketahanan 
yang relatif baik. Data yang dirilis oleh Badan Pusat 
Statistik 
(BPS) 
mencatat 
pertumbuhan 
ekonomi 
Indonesia pada tahun 2024 mencapai 5,03% secara 
tahunan (C-to-C), mencerminkan stabilitas di tengah 
berbagai tekanan eksternal dan domestik. Sektor jasa 
menjadi penopang utama pertumbuhan dengan kenaikan 
signifikan sebesar 9,80%, sementara konsumsi lembaga 
non-profit yang melayani rumah tangga (PK-LNPRT) 
mengalami pertumbuhan tertinggi sebesar 12,48%, 
didorong oleh peningkatan belanja sosial dan program 
kesejahteraan yang dikeluarkan pemerintah.
Dari sisi perdagangan internasional, Indonesia mencatat 
surplus perdagangan sebesar 31,04 miliar dolar AS 
pada tahun 2024, yang merupakan angka terendah 
dalam empat tahun terakhir. Penurunan ini terjadi 
akibat meningkatnya impor bahan baku dan barang 
modal sebesar 5,31%, yang mencerminkan tingginya 
permintaan domestik untuk kebutuhan industri, serta 
pelemahan ekspor di sektor pertambangan yang 
terdampak oleh fluktuasi harga komoditas global. 
Meskipun ekspor masih mengalami peningkatan sebesar 
2,29%, kenaikan impor yang lebih cepat menunjukkan 
bahwa permintaan domestik tetap tumbuh.
NATIONAL MACROECONOMIC REVIEW
Amid an uncertain global situation, Indonesia’s economy 
has remained relatively resilient. Data from the Central 
Statistics Agency (BPS) shows that Indonesia’s 
economic growth in 2024 reached 5.03% year-on-year 
(C-to-C), reflecting stability despite various external and 
domestic pressures. The services sector was the main 
driver of growth, with a significant increase of 9.80%, and 
consumption by non-profit institutions serving households 
(PK-LNPRT) saw the highest growth at 12.48%, driven 
by increased social spending and government welfare 
programs.
In international trade, Indonesia recorded a surplus of 
31.04 billion USD in 2024, the lowest figure in the past 
four years. This decline was due to a 5.31% increase in 
imports of raw materials and capital goods, reflecting high 
domestic demand for industrial needs, and a slowdown 
in mining exports impacted by global commodity price 
fluctuations. Although exports grew by 2.29%, the faster 
rise in imports indicates that domestic demand continues 
to grow.

Management Report
Inflasi pada tahun 2024 relatif terkendali dengan 
angka tahunan sebesar 1,57%, meskipun terdapat 
perbedaan signifikan antar wilayah. Faktor utama yang 
memengaruhi inflasi adalah kenaikan harga barang 
kebutuhan pokok, terutama makanan dan minuman, 
serta lonjakan biaya jasa lainnya seperti perawatan 
pribadi yang meningkat hingga 7,02%. Perbedaan inflasi 
antar daerah mendorong kebijakan ekonomi nasional 
yang lebih fleksibel, termasuk penyesuaian subsidi energi 
di wilayah dengan inflasi tinggi serta penguatan program 
bantuan sosial guna menjaga daya beli masyarakat yang 
terdampak lebih besar.
Dalam menghadapi tekanan eksternal, kebijakan moneter 
yang diambil oleh Bank Indonesia turut berkontribusi 
dalam menjaga stabilitas ekonomi nasional. Salah satu 
tantangan utama tahun ini adalah fluktuasi nilai tukar 
Rupiah terhadap Dolar AS. Sepanjang tahun, nilai tukar 
Rupiah mengalami pergerakan signifikan, dengan nilai 
tertinggi pada 2 Januari 2024 sebesar Rp15.516,19 
per dolar AS dan nilai terendah pada 27 Juni 2024 
sebesar Rp16.517,17 per dolar AS. Rata-rata nilai tukar 
sepanjang tahun berada pada angka Rp16.092,06 
untuk kurs jual dan Rp15.931,94 untuk kurs beli, lebih 
lemah dibandingkan asumsi dalam RAPBN 2024 yang 
memperkirakan rentang Rp14.700–Rp15.300 per dolar 
AS.
Bank Indonesia melakukan berbagai langkah intervensi 
guna menjaga stabilitas makroekonomi, termasuk 
kebijakan suku bunga dan penggunaan cadangan 
devisa. Depresiasi Rupiah memberikan tantangan bagi 
sektor industri yang bergantung pada bahan baku impor, 
namun juga membuka peluang bagi daya saing ekspor. 
Bank Indonesia juga melakukan operasi moneter untuk 
meredam volatilitas nilai tukar, termasuk intervensi 
langsung di pasar valas dan pengelolaan cadangan 
devisa.
Sejalan dengan upaya menjaga stabilitas nilai tukar, 
kebijakan suku bunga yang diterapkan Bank Indonesia 
turut menjadi faktor kunci dalam pengelolaan ekonomi 
makro. Pada awal tahun 2024, Bank Indonesia masih 
mempertahankan kebijakan suku bunga yang relatif 
ketat dengan BI 7-Day Reverse Repo Rate berada di 
level 6,00%. Namun, dalam Rapat Dewan Gubernur 
Januari 2025, Bank Indonesia menurunkan suku bunga 
acuan sebesar 25 basis poin menjadi 5,75% sebagai 
langkah untuk mendukung pertumbuhan ekonomi.
Inflation in 2024 remained relatively under control, 
with an annual rate of 1.57%, although there were 
significant differences between regions. The main 
factors driving inflation were rising prices of essential 
goods, especially food and beverages, and service 
costs, such as personal care, which rose by 7.02%. 
The inflation differences between regions led to 
more flexible national economic policies, including 
adjustments to energy subsidies in high-inflation 
areas and strengthening social assistance programs 
to help maintain the purchasing power of affected 
communities.
In response to external pressures, the monetary 
policies implemented by Bank Indonesia have helped 
maintain national economic stability. One of the 
main challenges this year was the fluctuation of the 
Rupiah against the US Dollar. Throughout the year, 
the exchange rate of the Rupiah saw significant 
movement, with the highest rate on January 2, 2024, 
at Rp15,516.19 per US Dollar and the lowest on June 
27, 2024, at Rp16,517.17 per US Dollar. The average 
exchange rate for the year was Rp16,092.06 for the 
selling rate and Rp15,931.94 for the buying rate, 
which was weaker than the assumption in the 2024 
State Budget, which projected a range of Rp14,700 to 
Rp15,300 per US Dollar.
Bank Indonesia has taken several intervention 
actions to maintain macroeconomic stability, including 
adjusting interest rates and using foreign exchange 
reserves. The depreciation of the Rupiah presents 
challenges for industries reliant on imported raw 
materials but also creates opportunities to boost 
export competitiveness. Bank Indonesia has also 
carried out monetary operations to reduce exchange 
rate volatility, including direct interventions in the 
foreign exchange market and managing foreign 
exchange reserves.
In line with efforts to maintain exchange rate stability, 
the interest rate policy implemented by Bank Indonesia 
has been a key factor in managing the macroeconomy. 
At the beginning of 2024, Bank Indonesia maintained 
a relatively tight interest rate policy, with the BI 7-Day 
Reverse Repo Rate set at 6.00%. However, during 
the January 2025 Board of Governors meeting, Bank 
Indonesia reduced the benchmark interest rate by 25 
basis points to 5.75% to support economic growth.

Dari sisi fiskal, APBN 2024 mencerminkan strategi 
pemerintah dalam menjaga keseimbangan antara 
belanja dan pendapatan negara. Fokus utama kebijakan 
fiskal pada tahun ini adalah percepatan transformasi 
ekonomi melalui penguatan sektor hilirisasi, transisi 
energi hijau, serta reformasi sistem perpajakan. 
Pemerintah juga terus menggenjot belanja infrastruktur 
untuk mendukung pertumbuhan ekonomi jangka panjang 
serta meningkatkan daya saing industri domestik.
Secara keseluruhan, perekonomian Indonesia pada 
tahun 2024 tetap tumbuh stabil di tengah berbagai 
tekanan global dan domestik. Sektor pertambangan, 
manufaktur, dan ekspor komoditas menjadi sektor 
yang paling terdampak oleh ketidakpastian global. 
Meskipun terdapat tekanan dari faktor eksternal, 
kombinasi kebijakan moneter yang adaptif dan strategi 
fiskal yang pro-pertumbuhan memungkinkan Indonesia 
untuk menjaga momentum pemulihan ekonomi serta 
memperkuat 
fundamentalnya 
dalam 
menghadapi 
tantangan di tahun 2025.
TINJAUAN INDUSTRI KONSTRUKSI NASIONAL
Industri konstruksi Indonesia pada tahun 2024 memainkan 
peran yang sangat signifikan dalam mendukung 
pertumbuhan ekonomi nasional. Berdasarkan data yang 
dirilis oleh Badan Pusat Statistik (BPS) dalam laporan 
“Konstruksi dalam Angka 2024,” sektor ini menyumbang 
sekitar 10,09% terhadap Produk Domestik Bruto (PDB) 
Indonesia sepanjang tahun tersebut[1]. Angka ini 
menunjukkan bahwa konstruksi tetap menjadi salah satu 
pilar utama pembangunan ekonomi di tengah berbagai 
tantangan global dan domestik.
Sejak awal tahun, dinamika industri konstruksi telah 
dipengaruhi oleh berbagai faktor, termasuk kebijakan 
pemerintah, perkembangan harga bahan bangunan, 
serta pergerakan investasi swasta dan asing. Pemerintah 
Indonesia, melalui Kementerian Pekerjaan Umum dan 
Perumahan Rakyat (PUPR), telah menetapkan anggaran 
infrastruktur sebesar Rp423,4 triliun, dengan alokasi 
sebesar Rp146,98 triliun secara khusus untuk proyek-
proyek yang dikelola oleh kementerian tersebut[2]. 
Fokus utama dari belanja infrastruktur ini mencakup 
pembangunan jalan tol, jembatan, bendungan, serta 
proyek pembangunan Ibu Kota Negara (IKN) Nusantara 
yang menjadi salah satu inisiatif strategis pemerintahan.
From a fiscal perspective, the 2024 State Budget (APBN) 
reflects the government’s strategy to maintain a balance 
between national spending and revenue. The main 
focus of fiscal policy this year is to accelerate economic 
transformation through strengthening the downstream 
sector, transitioning to green energy, and reforming 
the tax system. The government is also increasing 
infrastructure spending to support long-term economic 
growth and enhance the competitiveness of domestic 
industries.
Overall, Indonesia’s economy in 2024 remained stable 
despite various global and domestic pressures. The 
mining, manufacturing, and commodity export sectors 
were the most affected by global uncertainties. Although 
external factors posed challenges, adaptive monetary 
policies, and growth-oriented fiscal strategies allowed 
Indonesia to maintain economic recovery momentum 
and strengthen its fundamentals in preparation for 
challenges in 2025.
NATIONAL CONSTRUCTION INDUSTRY OVERVIEW
In 2024, Indonesia’s construction industry played a 
crucial role in supporting national economic growth. 
According to data from the Central Statistics Agency 
(BPS) in the “Construction in Figures 2024” report, 
the sector contributed about 10.09% to Indonesia’s 
Gross Domestic Product (GDP) that year. This figure 
highlights that construction remains one of the key pillars 
of economic development, despite various global and 
domestic challenges.
Since the beginning of the year, the dynamics of the 
construction industry have been influenced by various 
factors including government policies, changes in 
building material prices, and the movement of private 
and foreign investments. The Indonesian government, 
through the Ministry of Public Works and Public Housing 
(PUPR), has set an infrastructure budget of Rp423.4 
trillion, with Rp146.98 trillion specifically allocated for 
projects managed by the ministry. The main focus of 
this infrastructure spending includes the construction of 
toll roads, bridges, dams, and the development of the 
new capital city, Nusantara, one of the government’s key 
strategic initiatives.

Berdasarkan laporan “Laporan Kebijakan Moneter 
Triwulan IV-2024” yang diterbitkan oleh Bank Indonesia, 
pertumbuhan ekonomi nasional pada tahun 2024 
mencapai 5,03%, dengan sektor konstruksi mengalami 
pertumbuhan sebesar 7,02% dibandingkan tahun 
sebelumnya[3]. Pembangunan infrastruktur menjadi 
pendorong utama, terutama dengan adanya proyek-
proyek besar seperti Tol Trans-Sumatera dan Pelabuhan 
Patimban.
Namun, 
industri 
ini 
juga 
menghadapi 
berbagai 
tantangan. Laporan “Indeks Harga Perdagangan Besar 
2024” menunjukkan bahwa harga bahan bangunan 
mengalami kenaikan sebesar 0,72% secara tahunan 
(yoy), dipengaruhi oleh fluktuasi harga semen, pasir, 
batu fondasi, dan aspal[4]. Selain itu, kenaikan suku 
bunga global serta ketidakpastian geopolitik telah 
memberikan tekanan pada biaya material impor, yang 
semakin meningkatkan harga konstruksi.
Salah satu aspek menarik dalam industri konstruksi 
tahun 2024 adalah akselerasi digitalisasi dan inovasi 
teknologi. Dalam gelaran “Konstruksi Indonesia 2024,” 
yang diselenggarakan oleh Kementerian PUPR pada 
bulan November, tema utama yang diangkat adalah 
“Agility dan Adaptability Sektor Konstruksi yang Berdaya 
Saing.” Salah satu inovasi utama yang diperkenalkan 
adalah penggunaan Building Information Modeling 
(BIM), yang semakin banyak diterapkan dalam proyek-
proyek berskala besar untuk meningkatkan efisiensi dan 
transparansi konstruksi[5].
Pada akhir tahun, sektor konstruksi tetap menjadi salah 
satu motor penggerak pertumbuhan ekonomi Indonesia. 
Dengan anggaran besar yang dialokasikan pemerintah 
dan terus berkembangnya teknologi konstruksi, industri 
ini telah membuktikan ketangguhannya meskipun 
menghadapi tantangan yang cukup besar.
Based on the “Quarter IV-2024 Monetary Policy Report” 
published by Bank Indonesia, the national economy 
grew by 5.03% in 2024, with the construction sector 
rising by 7.02% compared to the last year. Infrastructure 
development was the main driver of this growth, 
specifically due to large projects such as the Trans-
Sumatera Toll Road and Patimban Port.
However, the industry also encounters several challenges. 
The “2024 Wholesale Price Index Report” shows the 
prices of building materials rose by 0.72% year-on-year 
(yoy), driven by fluctuations in the prices of cement, 
sand, foundation stones, and asphalt. Additionally, the 
rise in global interest rates and geopolitical uncertainty 
have put pressure on the cost of imported materials, 
further increasing construction prices.
One of the notable aspects of the construction industry 
in 2024 is the acceleration of digitalization and 
technological innovation. At the “Konstruksi Indonesia 
2024”, organized by the Ministry of Public Works and 
Public Housing (PUPR) in November, the key theme was 
“Agility and Adaptability of the Competitive Construction 
Sector.” One of the key innovations introduced was 
the use of Building Information Modeling (BIM), which 
is increasingly being applied in large-scale projects to 
enhance efficiency and transparency in construction.
By the end of the year, the construction sector remained 
a key driver of Indonesia’s economic growth. With a large 
budget allocated by the government and the continuous 
development of construction technology, the industry 
has proven its resilience despite encountering significant 
challenges.

KONTRIBUSI WIKA BETON TERHADAP INDUSTRI 
KONSTRUKSI NASIONAL
PT Wijaya Karya Beton Tbk (WIKA Beton) tetap 
menunjukkan resiliensi dan dominasi di industri 
konstruksi nasional. Hal ini dibuktikan dengan keterlibatan 
perusahaan dalam berbagai proyek pembangunan 
strategis yang terus digalakkan oleh pemerintah. Dengan 
kapabilitas produksi yang luas, jaringan distribusi yang 
kuat, serta penerapan standar industri yang tinggi, 
WIKA Beton terus mendorong efisiensi dan efektivitas 
pembangunan nasional.
1.	 Penyedia Utama Beton Pracetak untuk Infrastruktur 
Nasional
Sebagai produsen beton pracetak terbesar di 
Indonesia, WIKA Beton memainkan peran kunci 
dalam proyek infrastruktur strategis nasional, 
termasuk pembangunan jalan tol, pelabuhan, 
bandara, jembatan, dan Ibu Kota Nusantara (IKN). 
Produk pracetak berkualitas tinggi dari WIKA Beton 
telah meningkatkan efisiensi waktu dan biaya 
konstruksi dalam berbagai proyek nasional. Selain 
itu, keterlibatan dalam proyek pengembangan energi 
dan transportasi, seperti kereta cepat, jalur LRT, 
dan pembangunan smelter, semakin mengukuhkan 
peran WIKA Beton dalam pertumbuhan ekonomi 
nasional.
Untuk memastikan pemerataan pembangunan 
infrastruktur, pada tahun 2024 WIKA Beton membagi 
area pemasaran dan penjualannya ke dalam tujuh 
Wilayah Penjualan (WP), yang mencakup seluruh 
Indonesia serta ekspansi ke pasar Asia Tenggara. 
Wilayah ini meliputi Sumatera, Jawa, Kalimantan, 
Sulawesi, Maluku, Papua, Bali, Nusa Tenggara, 
dan pasar luar negeri. Dengan cakupan luas ini, 
WIKA Beton memastikan distribusi produk yang 
lebih efektif serta meningkatkan aksesibilitas 
pelanggan di berbagai wilayah.
2.	 Inovasi dalam Teknologi Konstruksi dan Efisiensi 
Proyek
WIKA Beton terus mendorong efisiensi sektor 
konstruksi nasional melalui inovasi teknologi, yang 
meliputi beton modular pracetak dan digitalisasi 
konstruksi.
WIKA BETON’S CONTRIBUTION TO THE NATIONAL 
CONSTRUCTION INDUSTRY
PT Wijaya Karya Beton Tbk (WIKA Beton) continues 
showing resilience and leadership in the national 
construction industry. This is evident through the 
company’s involvement in various strategic development 
projects promoted by the government. With its extensive 
production capabilities, strong distribution network, and 
adherence to high industry standards, WIKA Beton 
consistently drives efficiency and effectiveness in 
national development.
1.	 Primary Provider of Precast Concrete for National 
Infrastructure
As the largest producer of precast concrete in 
Indonesia, WIKA Beton plays a key role in national 
strategic infrastructure projects, including the 
construction of toll roads, ports, airports, bridges, and 
the Nusantara Capital City (IKN). WIKA BETON’s 
high-quality 
precast 
products 
have 
improved 
construction time and cost efficiency in various 
national projects. Additionally, its involvement in 
energy and transportation projects of high-speed 
trains, LRT lines, and smelter development, further 
strengthens its role in supporting national economic 
growth.
To ensure the equitable distribution of infrastructure 
development, in 2024, WIKA Beton divided its 
marketing and sales areas into seven Sales Regions 
(WP), covering all of Indonesia and expanding into 
Southeast Asia. These regions include Sumatra, 
Jawa, Kalimantan, Sulawesi, Maluku, Papua, Bali, 
Nusa Tenggara, and international markets. With 
this broad coverage, WIKA Beton ensures more 
effective product distribution and improved customer 
accessibility across various regions.
2.	 Innovation in Construction Technology and Project 
Efficiency
WIKA Beton continues to drive efficiency in the 
national construction sector through technological 
innovations, including precast modular concrete and 
construction digitalization.

a.	 Pengembangan Teknologi Pracetak Modular 
Perusahaan mengembangkan sistem modular 
pracetak yang memungkinkan pembangunan 
infrastruktur 
lebih 
fleksibel, 
cepat, 
dan 
berkualitas tinggi. Teknologi ini telah diterapkan 
dalam proyek perumahan, infrastruktur energi, 
serta gedung bertingkat, memberikan solusi 
konstruksi yang lebih efisien.
b.	 Integrasi Digitalisasi dan Teknologi Cerdas
WIKA Beton mengadopsi Building Information 
Modeling (BIM) dan sistem berbasis Internet of 
Things (IoT) untuk meningkatkan pengelolaan 
proyek serta efisiensi rantai pasok. Digitalisasi ini 
membantu kontraktor dan pengembang dalam 
mempercepat proses konstruksi, mengurangi 
pemborosan 
material, 
serta 
meningkatkan 
ketepatan waktu proyek.
Perusahaan juga mengintegrasikan tiga aspek 
utama Engineering, Produksi, dan Instalasi, 
yang memungkinkan operational excellence 
dan efisiensi tinggi dalam seluruh lini bisnisnya.
3.	 Kontribusi terhadap Keberlanjutan dan Industri Hijau
Sejalan dengan tren pembangunan berkelanjutan, 
WIKA Beton berperan dalam mengurangi dampak 
lingkungan sektor konstruksi dengan menerapkan 
standar industri hijau dan inovasi material ramah 
lingkungan.
a.	 Pengembangan Beton Ramah Lingkungan 
WIKA 
Beton 
memperkenalkan 
Green 
Concrete, produk inovatif dengan jejak karbon

bahan

mengedepankan konsep Green Building dan 
Net Zero Emission 2030.
a.	 Development of Modular Precast Technology
The company has developed a modular precast 
system for more flexible, faster, and high-quality 
infrastructure construction. This technology 
has been applied in housing projects, energy 
infrastructure, and high-rise buildings, providing 
more efficient construction solutions.

of

and 
Smart

WIKA 
Beton 
adopts 
Building

Modeling (BIM) and Internet of Things (IoT)-

and supply chain efficiency. This digitalization 
helps contractors and developers speed up the

and improve project timelines.
The company also integrates three key aspects 
Engineering, 
Production, 
and 
Installation 
enabling operational excellence and high 
efficiency across all its business operations.

In line with the trend of sustainable development, 
WIKA Beton plays a role in reducing the 
environmental impact of the construction sector by 
applying green industry standards and innovative 
eco-friendly materials.

WIKA Beton introduces Green Concrete, an 
innovative product with a lower carbon footprint, 
the use of recycled materials, and improved 
material durability. This concrete supports 
projects that focus on Green Building concepts 
and the Net Zero Emission goal for 2030.

SASARAN MUTU PRODUKSI BETON
PT Wijaya Karya Beton Tbk (WIKA Beton) berkomitmen 
untuk menjaga standar kualitas produk guna mendukung 
proyek-proyek 
infrastruktur 
dan 
konstruksi 
yang 
berkelanjutan. Sasaran mutu produksi beton sepanjang

efisiensi produksi, inovasi teknologi, serta kepatuhan 
terhadap standar nasional dan internasional.
Beberapa prinsip utama yang diyakini dapat memberikan

biaya, kualitas, predictability, kehandalan, produktivitas, 
kesehatan, 
keselamatan, 
lingkungan, 
koordinasi, 
inovasi, reusability, dan relocatability. Dengan prinsip 
ini, pemerintah terus mendorong peningkatan kapasitas 
industri beton pracetak dan prategang nasional. Sesuai 
RPJMN 2020-2024, kebutuhan beton pracetak untuk 
pembangunan infrastruktur diperkirakan sebesar 132,12 
juta ton, sementara untuk pembangunan Ibu Kota 
Negara (IKN) diperkirakan mencapai 27,52 juta ton.

Efficiency 
and 
Carbon 
Emission

facilities. This initiative helps reduce fossil fuel 
energy consumption and supports Indonesia’s 
commitment to achieving carbon emission 
reduction targets.
Additionally, WIKA Beton is committed to 
applying sound and accountable financial 
management while strengthening strategic 
partnerships with business partners to create 
added value for all stakeholders.
Throughout 2024, WIKA Beton has continued to make a 
strong contribution to the national construction industry. 
By providing high-quality precast concrete, adopting

sustainable development, the company plays an active

strengthens its position as a leader in the concrete 
industry in Indonesia and Southeast Asia.
QUALITY TARGETS FOR CONCRETE PRODUCTION
PT Wijaya Karya Beton Tbk (WIKA Beton) is committed 
to maintaining high product quality standards to support 
sustainable infrastructure and construction projects. The 
production quality goals for concrete in 2024 focus on 
improving quality, production efficiency, technological 
innovation, and compliance with national and international 
standards.
Several key principles believed to provide a competitive 
advantage in this technology include time, cost, 
quality, predictability, reliability, productivity, health, 
safety, 
environment, 
coordination, 
innovation, 
reusability, and relatability. With these principles, 
the government continues the growth of the national 
precast and prestressed concrete industry. According 
to the 2020-2024 National Medium-Term Development 
Plan (RPJMN), the demand for precast concrete for 
infrastructure development is estimated to be 132.12 
million tons, while the demand for the Capital City Project 
(IKN) is estimated at 27.52 million tons.

causes of defects before the production process begins.

MANAJEMEN BAHAN BAKU
Sebagai produsen beton pracetak terkemuka di Indonesia, 
PT Wijaya Karya Beton Tbk (WIKA Beton) menerapkan 
strategi manajemen bahan baku yang terintegrasi guna 
memastikan ketersediaan material berkualitas tinggi, 
efisiensi rantai pasok, serta keberlanjutan operasional. 
Manajemen bahan baku yang efektif menjadi elemen 
krusial dalam mendukung target produksi dan kualitas 
produk sepanjang tahun 2024.
1.	
Standar Operasional dan Prinsip Prudent dalam 
Pengadaan Bahan Baku
Demi menjamin optimalitas harga dan mutu, 
WIKA Beton memproduksi beton sesuai dengan 
Standar Operasi Prosedur (SOP) berbasis ISO 
9001:2015. Dalam pemilihan dan pengadaan 
bahan baku, perusahaan menerapkan prinsip 
prudent, dengan mempertimbangkan ketelitian dan 
kebijaksanaan tinggi guna memastikan ketersediaan 
stok minimal yang memadai di setiap pabrik.
4.	 Compliance with Regulations and Safety
As part of good corporate governance, WIKA Beton 
ensures:
a.	 The implementation of the Occupational Health 
and Safety Management System (OHSMS) at 
all stages of production to protect workers and 
ensure operational safety.
b.	 Compliance with Environmental Regulations, 
by applying an ISO 14001-based production 
system to reduce the environmental impact of 
concrete production waste.
c.	
Regular Audits and Evaluations, by implementing 
periodic measurement and reporting systems to 
ensure quality targets are met and continuous 
improvement is achieved.
Throughout 2024, WIKA Beton set production goals 
focused on superior quality, operational efficiency, 
product innovation, and compliance with regulations 
and sustainability standards. By implementing modern 
technology and strengthening production standards, the 
company is committed to supporting the development of 
more efficient, environmentally friendly, and sustainable 
infrastructure.
RAW MATERIAL MANAGEMENT
As a leading precast concrete manufacturer in Indonesia, 
PT Wijaya Karya Beton Tbk (WIKA Beton) implements an 
integrated raw material management strategy to ensure 
the availability of high-quality materials, supply chain 
efficiency, and operational sustainability. Effective raw 
material management is a crucial element in supporting 
production targets and product quality throughout 2024.
1.	 Operational Standards and Prudent Principles in 
Raw Material Procurement
To ensure optimal pricing and quality, WIKA Beton 
manufactures concrete following Standard Operating 
Procedures (SOP) based on ISO 9001:2015. In the 
selection and procurement of raw materials, the 
company applies prudent principles, considering 
careful planning and high discretion to ensure 
sufficient minimum stock availability at each factory.

based on SOPs that account for durability, safety, 
and the specific properties of each material. This 
approach allows the company to maintain raw 
material quality throughout the production process 
while optimizing storage and distribution cost 
efficiency.
2.

To ensure production continuity, WIKA Beton 
collaborates with various suppliers/vendors who 
have passed a rigorous selection process based on 
performance, quality, delivery times, Occupational 
Health and Safety (OHS), and supply consistency. 
This policy aims to avoid reliance on a single supplier 
and maintain a stable supply of raw materials across 
all company factories.
As part of the WIKA Group, WIKA Beton continues 
to prioritize supply from its internal network, 
considering fair transactions and cost efficiency. 
Meanwhile, supplier diversification is carried out to 
ensure the stability of raw material prices and quality 
amidst market dynamics.
3.

implements a digital stock management system for

includes:

aggregates, 
fly 
ash, 
and 
slag, 
to 
reduce 
environmental impact and support the Net Zero 
Emission 2030 target.
c.	
Implementation of a circular water management 
system, by recycling production wastewater for 
reuse in concrete mixing and machine cooling.

STRATEGI BISNIS TAHUN 2024
PT Wijaya Karya Beton Tbk (WIKA Beton) terus 
mengembangkan strategi bisnisnya guna menghadapi 
dinamika pasar dan memperkuat daya saing di industri

saham serta pemangku kepentingan.
1.	 Ekspansi Pasar dan Penguatan Pangsa Pasar
WIKA Beton menargetkan peningkatan pangsa

BUSINESS STRATEGY IN 2024
PT Wijaya Karya Beton Tbk (WIKA Beton) continues 
to develop its business strategy to adapt to market 
dynamics and strengthen its competitiveness in both the 
national and international construction industries. The 
2024 business strategy focuses on market expansion, 
product diversification, digitalization, sustainability, and 
operational efficiency to ensure sustainable growth and 
increased value for shareholders and stakeholders.
1.	 Market Expansion and Market Share Strengthening
WIKA Beton aims to increase its market share 
through the following strategies:
a.	 Expansion 
into 
international 
markets, 
particularly 
Southeast 
Asia, 
by 
targeting 
strategic infrastructure projects.
b.	 Increasing the contribution of the private sector 
to reduce reliance on government infrastructure 
projects and expand involvement in the mining, 
energy, and real estate sectors.
c.	
Optimizing the distribution network through 
7 Sales Regions (WP) across Indonesia and 
strengthening a more efficient supply chain.
2.	
Product and Service Diversification
To meet the growing market demands, WIKA Beton 
is developing innovations in its products and services 
as follows:
a.	
The development of modular concrete products 
allows for greater efficiency in project completion 
time.
b.	
The launch of eco-friendly products, such as Self 
Healing Concrete, made from recycled materials to 
reduce carbon emissions.
c.	
Providing 
integrated 
construction 
solutions, 
including design, production, and installation of 
precast concrete, to enhance customer satisfaction.

Kinerja Operasi Per Segmen Usaha
Performance Review Per Business Segment
Perseroan mengoperasikan bisnisnya melalui tiga 
segmen usaha utama, yakni Segmen Beton, Segmen 
Quarry, dan Segmen Jasa. Kegiatan inti Perseroan 
terfokus pada Segmen Beton yang bertanggung jawab 
atas produksi beton pracetak dan Ready Mix. Sementara 
itu, Segmen Quarry, sebagai bagian dari strategi 
backward dalam proses produksi beton, melibatkan 
kegiatan penambangan dan produksi material seperti 
split, screen, dan sebagainya melalui tiga Crushing 
Plant yang dimiliki oleh Perseroan. Di sisi lain, Segmen 
Jasa, sebagai bagian dari strategi forward Perseroan, 
menawarkan jasa layanan untuk menunjang bisnis 
Perseroan.
Perseroan secara rutin mengevaluasi kinerja masing-
masing segmen guna mencapai pengelolaan sumber 
daya yang optimal. Hasil evaluasi tersebut tercermin 
dalam Laporan Keuangan Perseroan yang telah diaudit 
oleh Kantor Akuntan Amir Abadi Jusuf, Aryanto, Mawar 
& Rekan sesuai dengan pedoman PSAK 5 (Penyesuaian 
2015) mengenai Segmen Operasi.
Pada tahun 2024, analisis kinerja tiap segmen usaha 
Perseroan, terutama yang terkait dengan aspek produksi 
seperti proses, kapasitas, perkembangan, pendapatan, 
dan profitabilitas, akan diuraikan secara rinci melalui 
penjabaran sebagai berikut:
1.	 SEGMEN USAHA BETON
Dua kegiatan produksi utama yang dijalankan oleh 
Segmen Usaha Beton mencakup Beton Pracetak 
dan Beton Ready Mix. 
A.	 Beton Pracetak 
Perseroan memproduksi Beton Pracetak yang 
mencakup dua varian, yaitu beton pracetak 
putar dan beton pracetak non-putar. Untuk 
beton pracetak putar, proses produksinya 
mencakup persiapan cetakan, penulangan, 
pengecoran, 
penarikan 
tulangan 
baja 
prategang, 
dan 
pemadatan 
menggunakan 
sistem putar (spinning). Sementara itu, beton 
pracetak non-putar diproduksi melalui tahapan 
persiapan cetakan, penulangan, pengecoran, 
dan pemadatan menggunakan metode vibrasi 
(dengan vibrator eksternal atau internal).
The Company operates its business through three main 
business segments: the Concrete Segment, the Quarry 
Segment, and the Services Segment. The Company’s 
core activities focus on the Concrete Segment, which 
is responsible for the production of precast concrete 
and Ready Mix. Meanwhile, the Quarry Segment, as 
part of a backward integration strategy in the concrete 
production process, involves mining and producing 
materials such as split, screen, and others through the 
Company’s three Crushing Plants. On the other hand, 
the Services Segment, as part of the Company’s forward 
integration strategy, offers service solutions to support 
the Company’s business.
The Company regularly evaluates the performance of 
each segment to achieve optimal resource management. 
The results of this evaluation are reflected in the 
Company’s Financial Statements, which have been 
audited by Accounting Firm Amir Abadi Jusuf, Aryanto, 
Mawar & Partner in accordance with PSAK 5 (2015 
Adjustment) regarding Operating Segments.
In 2024, the performance analysis of each business 
segment, particularly related to production aspects such 
as processes, capacity, developments, revenue, and 
profitability, will be elaborated in detail as follows:
1.	 CONCRETE BUSINESS SEGMENT
The two main production activities carried out by 
the Concrete Business Segment include Precast 
Concrete and Ready-Mix Concrete.
A.	 Precast Concrete
The Company produces Precast Concrete 
in two variants: spun precast concrete and 
non-spun precast concrete. For spun precast 
concrete, the production process includes mold 
preparation, reinforcement, casting, prestressed 
steel tendon tensioning, and compaction using a 
spinning system. Meanwhile, non-spun precast 
concrete is produced through mold preparation, 
reinforcement, casting, and compaction using 
vibration methods (with external or internal 
vibrators).

B.	 Beton Ready Mix 
Dalam 
mendiversifikasi 
produk 
guna 
mendukung berbagai proyek pembangunan 
infrastruktur, Perseroan juga menghasilkan 
Ready Mix Concrete sebagai bagian dari unit 
bisnisnya. Unit bisnis ini telah dibentuk untuk 
melengkapi produksi Beton Pracetak dengan 
menggunakan metode mobile plant, seperti 
mobile plant yang memproduksi berbagai jenis 
beton pracetak, termasuk tetrapod, U-Ditch, 
concrete barrier, dan produk beton lainnya yang 
bersifat nonstressing. 
Pendekatan ini diharapkan dapat menjadi 
alternatif terhadap metode stationary plant 
yang 
sudah 
dikembangkan 
sebelumnya. 
Ready Mix, sebagai produknya, dikembangkan 
dengan dukungan tenaga kerja profesional dan 
peralatan produksi yang mengadopsi teknologi 
terkini. Perseroan memasarkan Ready Mix 
dengan harga yang kompetitif, sehingga dapat 
hadir sebagai solusi pemenuhan kebutuhan 
beton di seluruh Indonesia.
Berikut adalah langkah-langkah dalam proses 
produksi Ready Mix:
Keterangan:
Description: 
Material Weighing: Proses penimbangan material alam dari bin material.
Material Weighing: The process of weighing natural materials from the material bin.
Material Loading: Proses loading material dari bin material ke mesin mixer.
Material Loading: The process of loading materials from the material bin into the mixer machine.
Concrete Mixing: Proses mixing semua material Pasir, Split, Semen, Air dan Additive menggunakan mesin mixer.
Concrete Mixing: Mixing all materials sand, gravel, cement, water, and additives using a mixer machine.
Concrete Loading: Proses pengangkutan Beton Ready Mix hasil mixing dengan menggunakan truck mixer.
Concrete Loading: The process of transporting ready-mix concrete, produced from mixing, using a mixer truck.
B.	 Ready-Mix Concrete
To diversify its products and support various 
infrastructure 
development 
projects, 
the 
Company also produces Ready-Mix Concrete 
as part of its business unit. This business unit 
has been established to complement Precast 
Concrete production by utilizing a mobile plant 
method, such as mobile plants that produce 
various types of precast concrete, including 
tetrapods, U-ditches, concrete barriers, and 
other non-stressing concrete products. 
This approach is expected to serve as an 
alternative to the previously developed stationary 
plant method. Ready-Mix, as the product, is 
developed with the support of professional labor 
and production equipment that adopts the latest 
technology. The Company markets Ready-Mix 
at competitive prices, ensuring it serves as a 
concrete supply solution throughout Indonesia.
Below are the steps in the Ready-Mix production 
process:

Strategi Segmen Beton Tahun 2024
Berikut adalah beberapa kebijakan strategis yang 
diterapkan oleh Segmen Beton pada tahun 2024 untuk 
meningkatkan kinerja produksi dan produktivitasnya:
1.	
Peningkatan 
produktivitas 
yang 
berwawasan 
lingkungan dengan menggunakan energi terbarukan 
melalui penggunaan solar cell;

cetakan dengan menggunakan sistem non baut 
(clip), magnet dan connector ring;

sarana dan prasarana jalur produksi pipa centrifugal.

Concrete Segment Strategy for 2024
The following are several strategic policies implemented 
by the Concrete Segment in 2024 to enhance production 
performance and productivity:
1.	
Environmentally Friendly Production Activities by 
utilizing renewable energy through the use of solar 
cells.
2.	
Strengthening Human Resources in the precast 
concrete industry through soft skills and hard skills 
training.
3.	
Innovation Based on Value Engineering and/
or IT in Quality Excellence Activities, including 
the application of AI Productivity such as Vision 
Intelligence (VI) and Load Scanner.
4.	
Production Line Flexibility by developing facilities 
and infrastructure for the centrifugal pipe production 
line.
In 2024, the Company’s concrete segment production 
capacity reached 10,62 million tons, an increase from 
10.97 million tons in 2023. This growth reflects the 
Company’s improved readiness to meet market demand, 
especially for infrastructure projects.
The capacity of precast concrete was recorded at 5.08 
million tons, showing a slight increase from the previous 
year. Meanwhile, ready-mix concrete experienced 
a decline to 5.55 million tons from 5.96 million tons 
previously, in line with rising demand across various 
regions.
Overall, production capacity has continued to grow 
over the past five years, from 7.53 million tons in 2020 
to 10,62 million tons in 2024, indicating the Company’s 
operational expansion and increased efficiency.

Pada tahun 2024, hasil segmen mengalami kenaikan 
sebesar 14,10%, dari Rp3,72 triliun di tahun 2023 menjadi 
Rp4,25 triliun di tahun 2024. Ini mengindikasikan bahwa 
profitabilitas operasional segmen beton tetap tumbuh. 
Selain itu, laba bersih segmen beton tercatat sebesar 
Rp54,28 miliar, meningkat 214,23% dibandingkan tahun 
2023 yang sebesar Rp17,28 miliar. Peningkatan ini 
menunjukkan bahwa meskipun beban pokok penjualan 
naik, pendapatan yang diperoleh masih mampu menutupi 
kenaikan biaya produksi, sehingga profitabilitas tetap 
terjaga.
2.	
SEGMEN USAHA QUARRY
Melalui 
Segmen 
Usaha 
Quarry, 
Perseroan 
menjalankan kegiatan produksi yang mencakup 
kegiatan 
penambangan 
batu 
andesit 
untuk 
memproduksi material split, screening, abu batu 
dan turunannya. Produksi dilakukan melalui 3 (tiga) 
Crushing Plant Perseroan, yaitu:
1.	
Crushing Plant Bogor;
2.	
Crushing Plant Lampung Selatan;
3.	
Crushing Plant Donggala. 
Dibentuk untuk mendukung bisnis di sektor hulu 
industri Pracetak Beton dan konstruksi, Crushing 
Plant 
menghasilkan 
produk 
yang 
bertujuan 
memenuhi kebutuhan material alam, seperti batu 
mineral alam yang dipecah menjadi batu split 
(dengan ukuran 1-2 dan 2-3 cm), screening, abu 
batu, dan material untuk kebutuhan pondasi jalan 
raya seperti agregat (kelas A dan kelas B). 
Crushing Plant Perseroan dapat menghasilkan 
produk 
yang 
seragam 
dan 
kubikal. 
Guna 
mengoptimalkan potensi, Perseroan menambah 
fasilitas laboratorium agregat dan pelabuhan, seperti 
yang dilakukan di Crushing Plant Lampung Selatan, 
sehingga dapat menjangkau pasar yang lebih besar 
di seluruh Indonesia.
In 2024, the segment’s results increased by 14.10%, 
from Rp3.72 trillion in 2023 to Rp4.25 trillion in 2024. This 
indicates that the operational profitability of the Concrete 
Segment continues to grow. Additionally, the segment’s 
net profit was recorded at Rp54.28 billion, reflecting a 
214.23% increase compared to Rp17.28 billion in 2023. 
This growth indicates that despite the rise in the cost of 
goods sold, the revenue generated was still sufficient 
to cover the increase in production costs, ensuring that 
profitability remained stable.
2.	
QUARRY BUSINESS SEGMENT
Through the Quarry Business Segment, the Company 
carries out production activities, including andesite 
stone mining to produce split stone, screening, stone 
dust, and their derivatives. Production is conducted 
through the Company’s three Crushing Plants, 
namely:
1.	 Crushing Plant Bogor
2.	 Crushing Plant South Lampung
3.	 Crushing Plant Donggala
Established to support upstream business in the Precast 
Concrete and construction industries, the Crushing Plant 
produces materials to meet the demand for natural stone, 
such as crushed mineral stone processed into split stone 
(sizes 1-2 cm and 2-3 cm), screening, stone dust, and 
materials for road foundation needs such as aggregate 
(Class A and Class B).
The Company’s Crushing Plants are capable of producing 
uniform and cubical-shaped products. To maximize its 
potential, the Company has added aggregate laboratory 
and port facilities, such as those implemented at Crushing 
Plant South Lampung, enabling broader market reach 
across Indonesia.

Keterangan: 
1.	 Drilling: proses pengeboran pada batuan untuk 
membentuk lubang bahan peledak.
2.	 Pengangkutan Bahan Peledak: proses pengangkutan 
bahan peledak yang telah ditentukan jumlah dan 
kebutuhannya, dari gudang penyimpanan menuju 
lokasi peledakan (blasting) sesuai prosedur yang 
terjamin keamanannya.
3.	 Perakitan Rangkaian Bahan Peledak: proses 
merangkai bahan peledak yang telah dimasukkan 
ke dalam lubang bor menggunakan kabel dan 
detonator. 
4.	 Blasting: 
proses 
peledakan 
batuan 
dengan 
rangkaian bahan peledak pada area yang telah 
ditentukan untuk memecah dan mengurai batuan 
berukuran masif menjadi raw material berukuran 
lebih kecil. 
5.	 Loading: proses pengangkutan raw material hasil 
blasting dengan menggunakan excavator ke dalam 
kendaraan angkut (dumptruck).
6.	 Hauling: proses pengangkutan raw material dengan 
menggunakan kendaraan angkut (dumptruck) dari 
lokasi loading menuju lokasi crusher.
Descriptions:
1.	
Drilling: The process of drilling rocks to create holes 
for explosives.
2.	
Explosives 
Transportation: 
The 
process 
of 
transporting predetermined amounts of explosives 
from the storage facility to the blasting site, following 
strict safety procedures.
3.	
Explosives Assembly: The process of assembling 
explosives inserted into boreholes using cables and 
detonators.
4.	
Blasting: The process of detonating explosives 
in designated areas to break down large rock 
formations into smaller raw materials.
5.	
Loading: The process of transporting raw materials 
from blasting sites into haul trucks using excavators
6.	
Hauling: The transportation of raw materials via haul 
trucks from the loading area to the crusher location

Hopper: The process of stockpiling raw materials 
into the hopper for crushing preparation.

Primary Jaw Crusher Process: The initial crushing 
of materials using a primary jaw crusher, producing 
stockpile stone and sirdam (a mix of sand and 
gravel).
9.	
Secondary Cone Crusher Process: The crushing of 
materials from the stockpile stone.
10.	 Tertiary Cone Crusher Process: The further crushing 
of materials from the secondary cone crusher, 
producing split stone, screening, and stone dust.

has fluctuated, reaching its peak in 2021 at 1.540.305 
m³. Nevertheless, the Company continues to maintain 
operational efficiency and ensure the availability of quarry 
materials to support ongoing construction projects.

3.	 SEGMEN USAHA JASA
Dalam menjawab tantangan pasar konstruksi 
di Indonesia yang menuntut solusi terintegrasi, 
Perseroan telah membentuk Segmen Bisnis Operasi 
Jasa untuk memberikan kemudahan dan kecepatan 
kepada pelanggan. Segmen ini merupakan bagian 
inti dari bisnis EPI (Engineering, Production & 
Installation), dengan spesialisasi dalam instalasi 
penunjang produk pracetak beton dan proyek 
pekerjaan sipil. 
Dengan lini bisnis ini, Perseroan mampu memahami 
perspektif dari dua sudut pandang, yaitu sisi produksi 
dan sisi pelanggan. Sehingga, Perseroan dapat 
terus bertransformasi menjadi entitas yang proaktif 
dalam memberikan layanan terbaik, mulai dari tahap 
Engineering, Produksi, Distribusi, hingga Instalasi 
terpasang, serta pelayanan after sales produk. 
Seluruhnya bertujuan untuk memberikan keyakinan 
kepada pelanggan terkait jaminan atas produk dan 
layanan Perseroan.
•	
Unit Jasa Pemancangan 
Untuk mendukung pemasangan produk tiang 
pancang pracetak beton, Perseroan telah 
membentuk Unit Jasa Pemancangan. Dengan 
menerapkan sistem produksi Jepang, Unit ini 
menggunakan Sistem Metode Inner Bore dan 
EASE (Earth Auger Slurry Excavation) Prebore 
yang ramah lingkungan. Sebagai pemegang 
lisensi 
pertama 
di 
Indonesia, 
Perseroan 
berupaya memaksimalkan daya dukung pondasi 
tiang pancang melalui kedua inovasi ini. 
Metode Inner Bore System merupakan cara 
pemasangan tiang pancang beton berdiameter 
besar dengan satu tahapan simultan antara 
penggalian dan penetrasi tiang pancang (one 
step simultaneous). Setelah itu, dilakukan 
proses solidifikasi atau pembentukan soket 
di ujung bawah tiang pancang dengan injeksi 
bahan semen sehingga diperoleh daya dukung 
ujung tiang pondasi yang optimal. 
3.	
SERVICE BUSINESS SEGMENT
In response to the challenges of the construction 
market in Indonesia, which demands integrated 
solutions, the Company has established the 
Service Operations Business Segment to provide 
convenience and speed for customers. This segment 
is an integral part of the EPI (Engineering, Production 
& Installation) business, specializing in supporting 
the installation of precast concrete products and civil 
construction projects.
Through this business line, the Company is able to 
understand perspectives from both the production 
and customer sides, allowing it to continuously 
transform into a proactive entity in delivering the best 
services—ranging from Engineering, Production, 
Distribution, and Installation, to after-sales service. 
All of these efforts aim to instill customer confidence 
in the Company’s products and services.
•	
Piling Services Unit
To support the installation of precast concrete 
piles, the Company has established the 
Piling Services Unit. By adopting a Japanese 
production system, this unit utilizes the Inner 
Bore Method System and EASE (Earth Auger 
Slurry Excavation) Prebore Method, which are 
environmentally friendly. As the first license 
holder in Indonesia, the Company strives to 
maximize the load-bearing capacity of pile 
foundations through these two innovative 
methods.
The Inner Bore Method System is a technique 
for installing large-diameter concrete piles 
through a one-step simultaneous process of 
excavation and pile penetration. Following this, 
a solidification process or socket formation 
is carried out at the bottom end of the pile by 
injecting cement-based materials, ensuring 
optimal end-bearing capacity for the foundation 
pile.

PT Wijaya Karya Beton Tbk

Profil Perusahaan

Sementara metode EASE Prebore adalah varian 
pengembangan dari metode pemasangan tiang 
pancang yang memanfaatkan Crane Pancang 
(Driving Rig) yang sama dengan metode Inner 
Bore, dengan penggantian attachment alat 
galinya. Prinsipnya, metode ini merupakan 
kombinasi antara metode perbaikan tanah 
DCM (Deep Cement Mixing) dan pondasi tiang 
pancang (Spun Pile).
•	
Unit Penunjang Konstruksi (Post Tension, 
Heavy Lifting, SHMS) 
Pada semester kedua tahun 2020, Unit 
Penunjang Konstruksi memperluas cakupan 
bisnisnya dengan memasuki ranah instalasi 
monitoring kesehatan struktur atau dikenal 
sebagai SHMS (Structural Health Monitoring 
System). Unit ini khususnya ahli dalam 
menerapkan sistem prestress pasca-tegang 
pada struktur pracetak beton dan bangunan 
sipil. 
Implementasinya 
melibatkan 
aplikasi 
SHMS yang dapat digunakan untuk memantau 
kondisi kesehatan seluruh struktur bangunan 
sipil, 
termasuk 
jembatan, 
terowongan, 
bendungan, dan gedung. Tak hanya itu, Unit 
Penunjang 
Konstruksi 
juga 
menawarkan 
layanan pemasangan girder pracetak beton 
untuk komponen jembatan. Dengan dukungan 
dari tim profesional berpengalaman yang 
tersebar di beberapa kota besar di Indonesia, 
Unit Penunjang Konstruksi dapat memberikan 
pelayanan 
terbaiknya 
di 
seluruh 
wilayah 
operasional Perseroan di Indonesia.
•	
Unit-Unit Proyek 
Dengan tujuan untuk menjadikannya sebagai 
core business yang mampu mengakomodasi 
semua 
aspek 
dalam 
sektor 
konstruksi, 
Perseroan telah membentuk Unit Proyek-
Proyek. Ruang lingkup pekerjaan mencakup 
berbagai bidang seperti konstruksi infrastruktur 
jalan layang dan non layang, pembangunan 
gedung, pelabuhan, serta proyek-proyek di 
sektor industri dan pembangkit. Unit Proyek ini 
terdiri dari berbagai organisasi yang bertugas 
di 
wilayah 
operasional 
Perseroan 
untuk 
menangani proyek-proyek konstruksi sipil yang 
melibatkan komponen pracetak beton dengan 
tingkat kompleksitas atau spesialisasi tertentu.
Meanwhile, the EASE Prebore Method is a 
variation of the pile installation method that 
utilizes the same Driving Rig (Piling Crane) 
as the Inner Bore Method, but with a different 
excavation attachment. Essentially, this method 
is a combination of Deep Cement Mixing (DCM) 
technology and Spun Pile foundation installation.
•	
Construction Support Unit (Post-Tension, 
Heavy Lifting, SHMS)
In the second half of 2020, the Construction 
Support Unit expanded its business scope 
into structural health monitoring installation, 
known as SHMS (Structural Health Monitoring 
System). This unit specializes in the post-
tension 
prestressing 
system 
for 
precast 
concrete structures and civil buildings.Its 
implementation involves SHMS applications 
that can be used to monitor the structural health 
of civil engineering structures, including bridges, 
tunnels, dams, and buildings. Additionally, the 
Construction Support Unit provides installation 
services for precast concrete girders used in 
bridge components. Supported by a team of 
experienced professionals operating in major 
cities across Indonesia, the Construction 
Support Unit ensures the best service delivery 
across all of the Company’s operational areas.
•	
Project Units
With the aim of making it a core business capable 
of accommodating all aspects of the construction 
sector, the Company has established the 
Project Units. The scope of work includes 
various sectors such as: Elevated and non-
elevated 
infrastructure 
construction,Building 
construction, Port construction, Industrial and 
power plant projects. The Project Units consist 
of various organizations operating within the 
Company’s business areas, handling civil 
construction projects that involve precast 
concrete components with a certain level of 
complexity or specialization.

Strategi Segmen Jasa Tahun 2024 
Berikut adalah beberapa kebijakan strategis yang

Pada tahun 2024, kapasitas produksi segmen jasa 
tercatat sebanyak 14 proyek, mengalami penurunan 
signifikan dibanding tahun 2023 yang mencapai 234 
proyek. Penurunan ini disebabkan oleh penyesuaian 
strategi bisnis dan selektivitas proyek demi menjaga 
kualitas dan efisiensi pelaksanaan.
Dalam lima tahun terakhir, kapasitas produksi segmen 
jasa memang mengalami fluktuasi. Puncaknya terjadi 
pada tahun 2022 dan 2021 masing-masing sebesar 295 
proyek, sebelum akhirnya menurun tajam di tahun 2024. 
Perseroan terus berupaya menyesuaikan fokus bisnis 
jasa dengan kebutuhan pasar dan ketersediaan sumber 
daya yang ada.
In 2024, the production capacity of the service business 
segment was recorded at 14 project units, a significant 
decrease compared to 234 projects in 2023. This decline 
was due to strategic business adjustments and a more 
selective approach to project execution, focusing on 
quality and efficiency.
Over the past five years, the production capacity of the 
service segment has fluctuated. It peaked at 295 projects 
in both 2022 and 2021, before dropping sharply in 2024. 
The Company continues to align its service business 
focus with market needs and available resources.
Service Segment Strategy in 2024
The following are several strategic policies implemented 
by the Service Segment in 2024 to improve production 
performance and productivity:
1.	
Conducting 
comprehensive 
project 
selection 
analysis, covering legal, commercial, and technical 
aspects.
2.	
Maximizing projects that utilize existing resources, 
such as materials, equipment, and management.
3.	
Targeting National Strategic Projects.
4.	
Positioning Operational Units as profit centers.
5.	
Focusing on projects where the majority of products 
come from WIKA Beton’s own production (bundling).

SEGMEN GEOGRAFIS
Dalam rangka mengukur penetrasi pasar dan kinerja 
operasional, Perseroan telah melakukan pengelompokan 
berdasarkan segmen geografis, yang terdiri dari Pulau 
Jawa dan luar Pulau Jawa.
Informasi ini disusun untuk menunjukkan kontribusi 
aset dan hasil usaha dari setiap wilayah geografis. 
Dengan pendekatan ini, Perseroan dapat lebih efektif 
dalam merancang strategi bisnis yang sesuai dengan 
karakteristik pasar di masing-masing daerah, serta 
meningkatkan efisiensi operasional dan pertumbuhan 
yang berkelanjutan.
Strategi Segmen Geografis Tahun 2024
Berikut adalah beberapa kebijakan strategis yang 
diterapkan oleh Segmen Geografis pada tahun 2024 untuk 
meningkatkan kinerja produksi dan produktivitasnya:
a.	
Bersinergi dengan WIKA dan WTON Grup;
b.	
Meningkatkan sinergi Precaster Entitas Anak 
BUMN;
c.	
Aktif melakukan monitoring LPSE, E-katalog, dan 
E-proc;
d.	
Penetrasi pasar di area-area kunci termasuk IKN, 
Tol Sumatera, dan Tol Jawa.
e.	
Berfokus pada penciptaan proyek, proyek-proyek 
khusus, produk inovatif, bisnis baru, dan pasar baru.
f.	
Mengimplementasikan strategi pricing yang tepat;
g.	
Melakukan 
Project 
Selection 
dengan 
mempertimbangkan 
kondisi 
keuangan 
calon 
pelanggan;
h.	
Aktif 
melakukan 
monitoring

dan

PT. PLN (Persero);
i.	
Mengupayakan keunggulan mutu dan ketepatan 
jadwal sesuai kontrak;

GEOGRAPHICAL SEGMENTS
To measure market penetration and operational 
performance, 
the 
Company 
has 
categorized 
its 
operations based on geographical segments, consisting 
of Java Island and outside Java Island.
This information is structured to highlight the asset 
contribution 
and 
business 
performance 
of 
each 
geographical area. Through this approach, the Company 
can design more effective business strategies tailored 
to the market characteristics of each region, while 
also enhancing operational efficiency and ensuring 
sustainable growth.
Geographical Segment Strategy for 2024
The following are several strategic policies implemented 
by the Geographical Segment in 2024 to enhance its 
production performance and productivity:
a.	
Strengthening synergy with WIKA and WTON 
Group;
b.	
Enhancing 
collaboration 
with 
State-Owned 
Enterprises’ precaster subsidiaries;
c.	
Actively monitoring procurement platforms such as 
LPSE, E-catalog, and E-proc;
d.	
Market penetration in key areas including the IKN, 
Sumatra Toll Road, and Java Toll Road;
e.	
Focusing on project creation, niche projects, 
innovative products, new business, and new 
markets;
f.	
Implementing effective pricing strategies;
g.	
Conducting project selection with consideration of 
the prospective client’s financial condition;
h.	
Actively monitoring the absorption and planned 
issuance of Budget Allocations and Detailed 
Contracts from PT PLN (Persero);
i.	
Ensuring quality excellence and timely completion in 
accordance with contractual agreements;

Pendapatan Segmen Geografis dari Pulau Jawa
Pendapatan usaha dari Pulau Jawa pada tahun 2024 
mengalami pertumbuhan sebesar 17,81%, meningkat 
dari Rp2,23 triliun di tahun 2023 menjadi Rp2,63 triliun. 
Kenaikan ini mencerminkan peningkatan aktivitas proyek 
dan efisiensi operasional yang lebih baik. Pendapatan 
dari Pulau Jawa tetap menjadi kontributor utama, 
menyumbang sekitar 53,75% dari total pendapatan 
usaha Perseroan di tahun 2024. 
Pendapatan Segmen Geografis dari Luar Pulau Jawa 
Pendapatan usaha dari luar Pulau Jawa juga mengalami 
kenaikan sebesar 14,98%, dari Rp1,97 triliun di tahun 
2023 menjadi Rp2,26 triliun di tahun 2024. Peningkatan 
ini menunjukkan adanya pertumbuhan proyek di luar 
Pulau Jawa yang semakin kuat, didorong oleh ekspansi 
infrastruktur dan peningkatan permintaan di wilayah-
wilayah strategis. 
Profitabilitas Segmen Geografis dari Pulau Jawa
Laba tahun berjalan dari Pulau Jawa mencatat lonjakan 
signifikan sebesar 289,13%, meningkat dari Rp11,04 
miliar di tahun 2023 menjadi Rp42,98 miliar di tahun 
2024. Pertumbuhan ini mencerminkan keberhasilan 
dalam efisiensi biaya dan peningkatan realisasi proyek 
yang berdampak positif terhadap profitabilitas. 
Geographical Segment Revenue from Java Island
Business revenue from Java Island in 2024 grew by 
17.81%, rising from Rp2.23 trillion in 2023 to Rp2.63 
trillion. This growth reflects increased project activity 
and improved operational efficiency. Revenue from Java 
Island remains the primary contributor, accounting for 
approximately 53.75% of the Company’s total business 
revenue in 2024.
Geographical Segment Revenue from Outside Java 
Island
Business revenue from outside Java Island also 
increased by 14.98%, from Rp1.97 trillion in 2023 
to Rp2.26 trillion in 2024. This growth highlights 
expanding project development outside Java, driven by 
infrastructure growth and increasing demand in several 
strategic regions.
Geographical Segment Profitability from Java Island
Net profit from Java Island surged significantly by 
289.13%, increasing from Rp11.04 billion in 2023 to 
Rp42.98 billion in 2024. This rise reflects improved cost 
efficiency and higher project realization, contributing to 
stronger profitability.

Tinjauan Keuangan
Financial Overview
Dalam bagian Analisis dan Pembahasan Manajemen, 
Perseroan 
menyajikan 
evaluasi 
terhadap 
kinerja 
keuangan untuk periode yang berakhir pada 31 
Desember 
2024. 
Pembahasan 
mengenai 
kinerja 
keuangan PT Wijaya Karya Beton Tbk beserta entitas 
anaknya disajikan dengan mematuhi prinsip yang diatur 
dalam Standar Akuntansi Keuangan (“SAK”) Indonesia 
dan penjelasan yang terdapat pada Catatan atas 
Laporan Keuangan Konsolidasian, yang merupakan 
bagian integral dari Laporan Tahunan ini.
Pembahasan dan analisis berikut mengacu pada Laporan 
Keuangan Perseroan untuk tanggal dan tahun-tahun 
yang berakhir pada 31 Desember 2024 dan 2023 yang 
telah diaudit oleh Kantor Akuntan Publik Amir Abadi Jusuf, 
Aryanto, Mawar dan Rekan (a member of the RSM Network) 
dalam laporannya tertanggal 20 Maret 2025. 
Pada 31 Desember 2024, Akuntan Publik memberikan 
opini 
bahwa 
Laporan 
Keuangan 
Konsolidasian 
Perseroan PT Wijaya Karya Beton Tbk dan entitas 
anaknya telah disusun dengan wajar dalam semua aspek 
yang bersifat materi, sesuai dengan Standar Akuntansi 
Keuangan di Indonesia. Opini tersebut mencakup posisi 
keuangan konsolidasian, kinerja keuangan, dan arus kas 
konsolidasi untuk periode keuangan yang berakhir pada 
tanggal tersebut.
In the Management Analysis and Discussion section, the 
Company presents an evaluation of financial performance 
for the period ending December 31, 2024. The discussion 
on the financial performance of PT Wijaya Karya Beton 
Tbk and its subsidiaries is presented in compliance 
with the principles set forth in the Indonesian Financial 
Accounting Standards (“SAK”) and the explanations 
provided in the Notes to the Consolidated Financial 
Statements, which form an integral part of this Annual 
Report.
The following analysis and discussion refer to the 
Company’s Financial Statements for the years ending 
December 31, 2024, and 2023, which have been audited 
by the Public Accounting Firm Amir Abadi Jusuf, Aryanto, 
Mawar & Partners (a member of the RSM Network) in 
their report dated March 20, 2025.
As of December 31, 2024, the Public Accountant issued 
an opinion stating that the Consolidated Financial 
Statements of PT Wijaya Karya Beton Tbk and its 
subsidiaries were fairly presented in all material respects 
in accordance with Indonesian Financial Accounting 
Standards. This opinion covers the consolidated financial 
position, financial performance, and cash flows for the 
financial period ending on that date.

Pada tahun 2024, total aset Perseroan turun 5,73% atau 
Rp436,98 miliar, terutama karena penurunan aset lancar 
sebesar 10,38%, yang mencerminkan optimalisasi 
modal kerja. Sementara itu, aset tidak lancar naik tipis 
0.56%, menunjukkan investasi yang stabil.
Dari sisi liabilitas, terjadi penurunan 12.42% atau 
Rp497.64 miliar, terutama karena turunnya liabilitas 
jangka pendek sebesar 18,39%, yang mencerminkan 
pembayaran utang yang lebih baik. Namun, liabilitas 
jangka panjang naik 67,67%, menunjukkan peningkatan 
pendanaan jangka panjang untuk ekspansi.
Sementara itu, ekuitas naik 1,67% atau Rp60,66 miliar, 
mencerminkan kinerja keuangan yang lebih stabil dan 
peningkatan laba ditahan. Hal ini menunjukkan posisi 
keuangan yang lebih sehat dan kesiapan Perseroan 
dalam menghadapi tantangan ke depan. 
ASET
Pada akhir tahun 2024, total Aset Konsolidasian 
Perseroan 
mencapai 
Rp7,19 
triliun. 
Angka 
ini 
menunjukkan penurunan sebesar Rp436,98 miliar atau 
5,73% dibandingkan dengan tahun sebelumnya yang 
tercatat sebesar Rp7,63 triliun. Penurunan tersebut 
terutama disebabkan oleh berkurangnya jumlah aset 
lancar Perseroan selama tahun 2024.
In 2024, the Company’s total assets decreased by 5.73% 
or Rp436.98 billion, primarily due to a 10.38% decline 
in current assets, reflecting working capital optimization. 
Meanwhile, non-current assets increased slightly by 
0.56%, indicating stable investments.
On the liabilities side, there was a 12.42% decrease, 
equivalent to Rp497.64 billion, mainly driven by an 
18.39% reduction in current liabilities, which reflects 
improved 
debt 
repayment. 
However, 
non-current 
liabilities rose by 67.67%, indicating an increase in long-
term funding for expansion.
Meanwhile, equity grew by 1.67% or Rp60.66 billion, 
reflecting a more stable financial performance and 
increased retained earnings. This demonstrates a 
healthier financial position and the Company’s readiness 
to face future challenges.
ASET
At the end of 2024, the Company’s Consolidated Total 
Assets reached Rp7.19 trillion. This represents a 
decrease of Rp436,98 billion or 5.73% compared to the 
previous year, which was recorded at Rp7.63 trillion. The 
decline was primarily due to a reduction in the Company’s 
current assets during 2024.

Per 31 Desember 2024, Perseroan mencatatkan 
total Aset Lancar sebesar Rp3,93 triliun, mengalami 
penurunan sebesar Rp455,08 miliar atau 10,38% 
dibandingkan 
dengan 
tahun 
sebelumnya 
yang 
tercatat Rp4,38 triliun. Penurunan ini dipengaruhi oleh 
berkurangnya nilai piutang usaha, piutang retensi, 
piutang yang belum ditagih, dan piutang lain-lain seiring 
dengan telah tertagihnya piutang-piutang tersebut. 
Selain itu, penurunan pada tagihan bruto pemberi kerja 
sebesar 69,54% serta jumlah persediaan yang turun 
24,47% turut berkontribusi terhadap penurunan total 
Aset Lancar Perseroan.
As of December 31, 2024, the Company recorded Total 
Current Assets of Rp3.93 trillion, a decrease of Rp455.08 
billion or 10.38% compared to the previous year, which 
stood at Rp4.38 trillion. This decline was influenced by 
a reduction in trade receivables, retention receivables, 
unbilled receivables, and other receivables, as these 
receivables had been collected. Additionally, a 69.54% 
decrease in gross amounts due from customers and 
a 24.47% decline in inventory also contributed to the 
decrease in the Company’s Total Current Assets.

PT Wijaya Karya Beton Tbk
Laporan Tahunan 2024 Annual Report
Profil Perusahaan
Company's Profile
Tinjauan Pendukung Bisnis
Business Support Overview
Ikhtisar Kinerja
Performance Highlights
Laporan Manajemen
Management Report
Hingga 31 Desember 2024, Piutang Usaha-Bersih 
Perseroan tercatat sebesar Rp918,69 miliar, mengalami 
penurunan 
sebesar 
Rp39,29 
miliar 
atau 
4,10% 
dibandingkan dengan posisi per 31 Desember 2023 
yang mencapai Rp957,98 miliar. Penurunan ini terutama 
disebabkan oleh berkurangnya nilai piutang usaha dari 
pihak berelasi.
Piutang Usaha Pihak Berelasi-Bersih per 31 Desember 
2024 tercatat sebesar Rp417,84 miliar, turun Rp115,89 
miliar atau 21,71% dibandingkan tahun sebelumnya 
yang 
mencapai 
Rp533,73 
miliar. 
Penurunan 
ini 
dipengaruhi oleh telah tertagihnya piutang dari beberapa 
kerja sama operasi (KSO), antara lain KSO PT Hutama 
Karya (Persero) Tbk - PT Wijaya Karya (Persero) Tbk - 
PT Brantas Abipraya (Persero), KSO PT Hutama Karya 
(Persero) Tbk - PT Adhi Karya (Persero) - PT Brantas 
Abipraya (Persero), serta KSO PT Pembangunan 
Perumahan (Persero) Tbk - PT Nindya Karya.
Sementara itu, Piutang Usaha Pihak Ketiga-Bersih 
mengalami peningkatan, mencapai Rp500,85 miliar per 
31 Desember 2024, naik Rp76,60 miliar atau 18,05% 
dari Rp424,25 miliar pada tahun sebelumnya. Kenaikan 
ini terutama berasal dari peningkatan tagihan kepada 
beberapa mitra, termasuk KSO PT Hutama Karya 
(Persero) - PT Brantas Abipraya (Persero) - PT Jaya 
Konstruksi Manggala Pratama Tbk - PT Yasa Patria 
Perkasa, PT Jakarta Propertindo, dan PT Mitra Murni 
Perkasa.
As of December 31, 2024, the Company’s Net Trade 
Receivables were recorded at Rp918.69 billion, a 
decrease of Rp39.29 billion or 4.10% compared to 
Rp957.98 billion as of December 31, 2023. This decline 
was primarily due to the decrease in trade receivables 
from related parties.
Net Trade Receivables from Related Parties amounted 
to Rp417.84 billion, down by Rp115.89 billion or 21.71% 
from Rp533.73 billion in the previous year. This decline 
was influenced by the collection of receivables from 
several joint operations (KSO), including KSO PT Hutama 
Karya (Persero) Tbk - PT Wijaya Karya (Persero) Tbk - 
PT Brantas Abipraya (Persero), KSO PT Hutama Karya 
(Persero) Tbk - PT Adhi Karya (Persero) - PT Brantas 
Abipraya (Persero), and KSO PT Pembangunan 
Perumahan (Persero) Tbk - PT Nindya Karya.
Meanwhile, Net Trade Receivables from Third Parties 
increased to Rp500.85 billion as of December 31, 2024, 
up Rp76.60 billion or 18.05% from Rp424.25 billion in the 
previous year. This increase was primarily due to higher 
billing to several partners, including KSO PT Hutama 
Karya (Persero) - PT Brantas Abipraya (Persero) - 
PT Jaya Konstruksi Manggala Pratama Tbk - PT Yasa 
Patria Perkasa, PT Jakarta Propertindo, and PT Mitra 
Murni Perkasa.

As of December 31, 2024, the Company’s Advance 
Payments were recorded at Rp10.82 billion, a decrease 
of Rp5.10 billion or 32.05% compared to Rp15.93 billion 
in the previous year. This decline was mainly due to 
a reduction in advance payments to suppliers and a 
decrease in project prepayments in line with project 
completion progress.
(Dalam jutaan Rupiah l In million Rupiah)

Aset Pajak Tangguhan
Per 31 Desember 2024, Aset Pajak Tangguhan Perseroan 
tercatat sebesar Rp2,80 miliar, mengalami penurunan 
sebesar Rp6,32 miliar atau 69,29% dibandingkan dengan 
Rp9,12 miliar pada 31 Desember 2023. Penurunan ini 
terutama disebabkan oleh pelunasan kewajiban pajak 
yang dilakukan Perseroan pada periode sebelumnya, 
sehingga mengurangi saldo aset pajak tangguhan yang 
diakui.

Per 31 Desember 2024, Investasi Ventura Bersama 
tercatat sebesar Rp1,95 miliar, mengalami penurunan 
sebesar Rp1,53 miliar atau 43,97% dibandingkan dengan 
Rp3,48 miliar pada 31 Desember 2023. Penurunan ini 
disebabkan oleh distribusi keuntungan secara tunai 
dari KSO Wijaya Karya Beton – Emrail dan KSO Wijaya 
Karya Beton – Murni, serta proses penutupan KSO 
Wika Kobe – AJB – Sinarbali seiring dengan selesainya 
proyek kerja sama.
Properti Investasi
Per 31 Desember 2024, Properti Investasi Perseroan 
tercatat sebesar Rp191,56 miliar, meningkat Rp2,60 
miliar atau 1,37% dibandingkan tahun sebelumnya 
yang tercatat Rp188,96 miliar. Peningkatan ini terutama 
berasal dari penambahan properti investasi yang 
diperoleh melalui konversi sebagian piutang usaha WPG 
kepada PT Samudra Bangun Raya. Konversi tersebut 
dilakukan dalam bentuk aset berupa ruko yang berlokasi 
di Bogor, Jawa Barat, yang selanjutnya dicatat sebagai 
bagian dari portofolio properti investasi Perseroan.
Deferred Tax Assets
As of December 31, 2024, the Company’s Deferred Tax 
Assets were recorded at Rp2.80 billion, a decrease of 
Rp6.32 billion or 69.29% compared to Rp9.12 billion as of 
December 31, 2023. This decline was mainly due to the 
settlement of tax obligations carried out by the Company 
in the previous period, reducing the recognized balance 
of deferred tax assets.
As of December 31, 2024, the Company’s Joint Venture 
Investments were recorded at Rp1.95 billion, a decrease 
of Rp1.53 billion or 43.97% compared to Rp3.48 billion 
as of December 31, 2023. This decline was primarily due 
to cash profit distribution from KSO Wijaya Karya Beton 
– Emrail and KSO Wijaya Karya Beton – Murni, and the 
ongoing closure process of KSO Wika Kobe – AJB – 
Sinarbali following the completion of the project.
Investment Property
As of December 31, 2024, the Company’s Investment 
Property was recorded at Rp191.56 billion, an increase of 
Rp2.60 billion or 1.37% compared to the previous year’s 
Rp188.96 billion. This increase was primarily driven by 
the addition of investment properties acquired through 
the conversion of part of WPG’s trade receivables to 
PT Samudra Bangun Raya. The conversion was made 
in the form of a commercial shophouse asset located in 
Bogor, West Java, which was subsequently recorded as 
part of the Company’s investment property portfolio.
(Dalam jutaan Rupiah l In million Rupiah)

Aset Hak Guna-Bersih
Per 31 Desember 2024, Aset Hak Guna-Bersih 
Perseroan tercatat sebesar Rp7,48 miliar, mengalami 
peningkatan sebesar Rp99 juta atau 1,34% dibandingkan 
tahun sebelumnya yang tercatat Rp7,38 miliar. Kenaikan 
ini terutama disebabkan oleh penambahan aset hak 
guna atas bangunan yang digunakan untuk operasional 
kantor di WIKA Tower 1 serta Wilayah Penjualan di 
Sumatera Utara dengan perpanjangan hak guna untuk 
lokasi tersebut dilakukan setiap dua tahun sekali guna 
mendukung kelangsungan operasional Perseroan.
Aset Tetap-Bersih
Per 31 Desember 2024, Aset Tetap-Bersih Perseroan 
tercatat sebesar Rp3,01 triliun, meningkat Rp4,25 miliar 
atau 0,14% dibandingkan dengan Rp3 triliun pada 31 
Desember 2023. Kenaikan ini terutama disebabkan oleh 
tambahan investasi yang dilakukan Perseroan untuk 
memperluas fasilitas operasional, termasuk pengadaan 
peralatan dan cetakan yang mendukung proses produksi 
serta efisiensi kerja.
Investasi Jangka Panjang Lainnya
Investasi Jangka Panjang Lainnya sampai dengan 31 
Desember 2024 tercatat sebesar Rp2,50 miliar, tidak 
mengalami perubahan jika dibandingkan Rp2,50 miliar 
pada tahun sebelumnya.
Aset Tidak Lancar Lainnya
Per 31 Desember 2024, Aset Tidak Lancar Lainnya 
tercatat sebesar Rp50,87 miliar, naik Rp19 miliar atau 
59,65% dibandingkan Rp31,87 miliar pada tahun 
sebelumnya. Kenaikan tersebut terutama disebabkan 
oleh penempatan tambahan dana dalam bentuk rekening 
deposito yang merupakan fasilitas kredit dari PT Bank 
Negara Indonesia (Persero) Tbk.
Right-of-Use Assets - Net
As of December 31, 2024, the Company’s Right-of-Use 
Assets - Net were recorded at Rp7.48 billion, an increase 
of Rp99 million or 1.34% compared to the previous 
year’s Rp7.38 billion. This increase was mainly due to 
the addition of right-of-use assets for buildings used for 
office operations in WIKA Tower 1 and the Sales Region 
I in North Sumatra, with the extension of usage rights 
for these locations being renewed every two years to 
support the Company’s operational continuity.
Fixed Assets - Net
As of December 31, 2024, the Company’s Fixed Assets 
- Net were recorded at Rp3.01 trillion, an increase of 
Rp4.25 billion or 0.14% compared to Rp3 trillion as of 
December 31, 2023. This increase was primarily due 
to additional investments made by the Company to 
expand operational facilities, including the procurement 
of equipment and molds that support the production 
process and work efficiency.
Other Long-Term Investments
Other Long-Term Investments as of December 31, 2024, 
were recorded at Rp2.50 billion, showing no changes 
compared to Rp2.50 billion in the previous year.
Other Non-Current Assets
As of December 31, 2024, Other Non-Current Assets were 
recorded at Rp50.87 billion, an increase of Rp19 billion 
or 59.65% compared to Rp31.87 billion in the previous 
year. This increase was primarily due to additional fund 
placements in deposit accounts, which are part of a credit 
facility from PT Bank Negara Indonesia (Persero) Tbk.

LIABILITY
As of the end of 2024, the Company’s Consolidated 
Liabilities stood at Rp3.50 trillion, a decrease of Rp501.61 
billion or 12.52% from the previous year’s Rp4.01 trillion. 
This reduction was mainly driven by a decrease in short-
term liabilities, reflecting the Company’s enhanced ability 
to manage its financial obligations. 
The improvement in liability structure also contributed to 
a lower debt-to-equity ratio, indicating stronger financial 
health and improved capital stability.

Pada akhir tahun 2024, Liabilitas Jangka Pendek 
Perseroan tercatat sebesar Rp3,04 triliun, turun Rp685,67 
miliar atau 18,39% dibandingkan dengan Rp3,73 triliun 
pada tahun 2023. Penurunan ini terutama disebabkan 
oleh pelunasan pinjaman jangka pendek, pembayaran 
utang usaha kepada pihak ketiga, pembayaran utang 
pajak, serta pembayaran beban akrual. Langkah ini 
mencerminkan komitmen Perseroan dalam mengelola 
kewajiban keuangan secara efektif.
Pinjaman Jangka Pendek
Pada tahun 2024, tidak terdapat adanya pencatatan pinjaman 
jangka pendek. Hal ini disebabkan oleh telah terlunasinya 
pinjaman jangka pendek kepada PT Bank Mandiri (Persero) 
Tbk dan PT Bank Syariah Indonesia (Persero) Tbk.

Per 31 Desember 2024, Utang Usaha Perseroan tercatat 
sebesar Rp1,97 triliun, mengalami penurunan sebesar 
Rp85,16 miliar atau 4,14% dibandingkan dengan Rp2,06 
triliun pada 31 Desember 2023. Penurunan ini terutama 
disebabkan oleh pembayaran sebagian utang kepada 
pemasok atas pembelian bahan baku yang digunakan 
dalam 
pelaksanaan 
proyek, 
serta 
penyelesaian 
kewajiban kepada subkontraktor. Pengelolaan utang 
usaha yang lebih baik ini mencerminkan komitmen 
Perseroan dalam menjaga kesehatan keuangan dan 
hubungan kerja sama yang baik dengan mitra bisnis.
At the end of 2024, the Company’s Short-Term Liabilities 
were recorded at Rp3.04 trillion, a decrease of Rp685,67 
billion or 18,39% compared to Rp3.73 trillion in 2023. 
This decline was primarily due to the repayment of short-
term loans, payments to third-party trade payables, 
tax liabilities, and accrued expenses. This step reflects 
the Company’s commitment to managing its financial 
obligations effectively.
Short-Term Loans
In 2024, there were no recorded short-term loans. This 
was due to the full repayment of short-term loans to 
PT Bank Mandiri (Persero) Tbk and PT Bank Syariah 
Indonesia (Persero) Tbk.
As of December 31, 2024, the Company’s Trade 
Payables were recorded at Rp1.97 trillion, a decrease 
of Rp85.16 billion or 4.14% compared to Rp2.06 trillion 
as of December 31, 2023. This decline was primarily 
due to partial payments to suppliers for the purchase of 
raw materials used in project execution, as well as the 
settlement of obligations to subcontractors. Improved 
trade payable management reflects the Company’s 
commitment to maintaining financial health and fostering 
strong business relationships with its partners.

Per 31 Desember 2024, utang pajak Perseroan tercatat 
sebesar Rp65,09 miliar, turun signifikan sebesar Rp65,18
